class="ud-heading-md ud-form-label ud-heading-sm" for="form-group--1903">Overall explanation</label><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-text-md rt-scaffolding" id="overall-explanation">Docker uses layers to store intermediate build artifacts. Leveraging Docker's layer caching mechanism is crucial for optimizing build times in CI/CD pipelines. Layers are cached during successive builds, and if there are no changes to a particular layer, Docker can reuse the cached layer, significantly reducing build times.</div></div><div data-purpose="domain-pane" class="domain-pane--domain-pane--Pw9dK"><div class="domain-pane--domain-pane-header--2263m ud-heading-md">Domain</div><div class="ud-text-md">CI/CD Pipeline, Docker, Optimization</div></div></div></div></div></div></div>
